FNV PBR PPLIGHTING SHADER INPUT SIGNATURE FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which shader creation arguments identify the safe PPLighting families?
2. Which shader-interface apply path uploads constants before SetShaders?
3. Which texture-stage and sampler-state helpers are active for those passes?
4. What exact input/register/texture contract is still missing before visible replacement?

Compatibility rule:
Do not emit or bind a replacement BRDF shader until one family has proven input semantics, constants, texture stages, and fallback ownership.
